from googleapiclient.discovery import build
import io, os
from googleapiclient.http import MediaIoBaseDownload
from google.colab import auth
auth.authenticate_user()
drive_service = build('drive', 'v3')
results = drive_service.files().list(
    q="name = 'kaggle.json'", fields="files(id)").execute()
kaggle_api_key = results.get('files', [])

filename = "~/.kaggle/kaggle.json"
os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(filename), exist_ok=True)
request = drive_service.files().get_media(fileId=kaggle_api_key[0]['id'])
fh = io.FileIO(filename, 'wb')
downloader = MediaIoBaseDownload(fh, request)
done = False
while done is False:
    status, done = downloader.next_chunk()
    print("Download %d%%." % int(status.progress() * 100))
os.chmod(filename, 600)

images =  list(data_dir.glob("*.png"))
images = shuffle(images)

dataset_amount = len(images)

amount_train = int ( ( dataset_amount * perc_train ) / 100 )
amount_test  = dataset_amount - amount_train


images_train = images[:-amount_test]
images_test = images[-amount_test:]

print('Total de imagens : ' , dataset_amount + 1 , ' - Imagens para teste: ' , len(images_test) , ' - Imagens para treino: ' , len(images_train))


for file in images_train:
       shutil.move( str(file) , '/content/samples/train')
       label = file.name.split(".png")[0]
       for ch in label:
           characters.add(ch)

for file in images_test:
       shutil.move(str(file), '/content/samples/test')
       label = file.name.split(".png")[0]
       for ch in label:
           characters.add(ch)

for image in list(data_dir.glob("*.jpg")):
   shutil.move(str(image), '/content/samples/jpg')

print('Imagens separadas nas pastas /content/samples/train /content/samples/test e /content/samples/8n5p3')


# Reordenando os caracteres usados
characters = sorted(characters)

print(characters)

from keras import layers
from keras.models import Model
from keras.models import load_model
from keras import callbacks
import os
import cv2
import string
import numpy as np

# Definindo todos os "codigos" usados nos captcha
# symbols = string.ascii_lowercase + "0123456789" # All symbols captcha can contain

symbols = ''
for charac in characters:
    symbols = symbols + charac

num_symbols = len(symbols)
img_shape = (50, 200, 1)

Definição da função de criação do modelo

In [11]:
def create_model():
    img = layers.Input(shape=img_shape) 
    conv1 = layers.Conv2D(16, (3, 3), padding='same', activation='relu')(img)
    mp1 = layers.MaxPooling2D(padding='same')(conv1)  
    conv2 = layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), padding='same', activation='relu')(mp1)
    mp2 = layers.MaxPooling2D(padding='same')(conv2)  
    conv3 = layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), padding='same', activation='relu')(mp2)
    mp3 = layers.MaxPooling2D(padding='same')(conv3)  
    conv9 = layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), padding='same', activation='relu')(mp3)
    bn = layers.BatchNormalization()(conv9)
    mp9 = layers.MaxPooling2D(padding='same')(bn)
    
    # Pega um vetor e faz a criação de 5 camadas para a predição de 1 dos 5 caracteres
    flat = layers.Flatten()(mp9)
    outs = []
    for _ in range(5):
        dens1 = layers.Dense(64, activation='relu')(flat)
        drop = layers.Dropout(0.5)(dens1)
        res = layers.Dense(num_symbols, activation='sigmoid')(drop)

        outs.append(res)
    
    # Compilação e retorno do modelo 
    model = Model(img, outs)
    model.compile(loss='categorical_crossentropy', optimizer='adam',metrics=["accuracy"])
    return model

Definição da função de pré-processamento

In [12]:
def preprocess_data(type_process):
    if type_process == 'train':
       dir = dir_train
    else:
       dir = dir_test
    n_samples = len(os.listdir(dir))
    X = np.zeros((n_samples, 50, 200, 1)) 
    y = np.zeros((5, n_samples, num_symbols)) 

    for i, pic in enumerate(shuffle(os.listdir(dir))):
        # Lendo a imagem como um grayscale
        img = cv2.imread(os.path.join(dir, pic), cv2.IMREAD_GRAYSCALE)
        pic_target = pic[:-4]
        if len(pic_target) < 6:
            # Escalando e remodelando a imagem
            img = img / 255.0
            img = np.reshape(img, (50, 200, 1))
            # Definindo os destinos e codificando-os usando OneHotEncoding
            targs = np.zeros((5, num_symbols))
            for j, l in enumerate(pic_target):
                ind = symbols.find(l)
                targs[j, ind] = 1
            X[i] = img
            y[:, i] = targs
    
    # Retorno do dado final
    return X, y

# Realização de um processamento

X_train, y_train = preprocess_data('train')
X_test, y_test = preprocess_data('test')

Definição da função de predição

In [16]:
# Definição da função de predição
def predict(filepath):
    img = cv2.imread(filepath, cv2.IMREAD_GRAYSCALE)
    if img is not None:
        img = img / 255.0
    else:
        print("Not detected");
    res = np.array(model.predict(img[np.newaxis, :, :, np.newaxis]))
    # ans = np.reshape(res, (5, 36))
    ans = np.reshape(res, (5, num_symbols))
    l_ind = []
    probs = []
    for a in ans:
        l_ind.append(np.argmax(a))
        #probs.append(np.max(a))

    capt = ''
    for l in l_ind:
        capt += symbols[l]
    return capt#, sum(probs) / 5

# print(predict('/content/samples/8n5p3/8n5p3.png'))

for i, pic in enumerate(shuffle(os.listdir(dir_final))):
     predicao = predict(os.path.join(dir_final,pic))
     # print(pic , ' - predict: ' , predicao)
     _,ax = plt.subplots(1,1, figsize=(5,3))
     img = cv2.imread(str(os.path.join(dir_final,pic)))
     print(pic , pic.split(".png")[0] , ' - predict: ' , predicao)
     ax.imshow(img)
     ax.axis('off')
     plt.show()
